1.

I get up. The blanket fell.

There's a holey boot under the sofa,

And by the stove, a scarlet tree hung to the floor
An untidy clump of rags.

Outside the window - cheerful, wonderful and sunny
Day—in the morning—an incomprehensible joy.
For whom? For me? Complete, complete...
Nonsense. Doesn't matter. I don't need

I got dressed. I washed my face. Even in the mirror

It's someone not me—distorted

And the green one looked in and was endlessly frightened...

What - hungry? But it doesn't hurt.

And Filippov is surrounded by a bunch of -
Like a shameless drunk, I stagger along.

After all, I’m wearing boots and a leather jacket,

And in advance. shame is tormenting.

Or see the fractures of sympathies
A regretful nepman, an obese pig...
The looks of the girls are ‘kind... Let them be!
Let them look and admire me.

I'll go as if nothing happened
And, perhaps, I’ll take another puff of tobacco—
To get more, drunker...

So, I’m lying on the bed again and tired
I remember something, and I dream, and I get angry.

‚Evening around the city in the holes of the streets

Wet autumn climbed.
Here they flashed electricity,
The forest is bright and flashy,

I shuffle, I shuffle, I clean the panels,
I clean my birch bark boots.

There are many people walking in the night carousel,
On the birch bark of walking feet,

You need us, streets’ panel,

And to those who walk at night.

In our arms, like in a dead dream,
Everything dies before morning.

Hey, lord of the fields, city!
We are your inseparable part,
We revive the streets-holes.

We don't give it to you. miss.

Evening and night are work time.
Every day—evening and night.

No vacations, no absenteeism, no benefits
It is not given to us by ourselves or anyone.

Evening around the city in the holes of the streets
Wet and noisy climbed.
Oh, the walkers shook themselves,
lived signs forest.

HONEY DEPOSIT I.
+,

Life is good in Vedrine. The weather is sunny; along the banks of Opochenka
and Lopaeni dozens of springs are scattered; you look into another - how
you see yourself in the mirror, but in another it becomes cloudy, because all around
troublemaker grass grows.

And every spring has its own admirer: he understands and loves it,
removes stones.

Ivan Kamanin loved his relativescheck; sits next to him, puts him down
buckets on the grass, looks at the mountain, where the blue green alders and white
If the factory fences have grown in, he’ll think about it. I stopped in '18
calico stuffed, and people scattered to the grain stores. places, cities,
many went to the front. Ivan remained in Vedrine. Carried firewood to Med-
a wooden beam, laid out a fire under the boilers, watched how the white laugh-
the lime swelled with the tan; played songs, read newspapers - life was good,
On Saturdays he came home, washed in a public bath and until the evening
Chera smelled of birch steam. Ivan’s years are not old, only 39, but not
thought a lot...

So today I sat down over a spring; There are lush grasses all around, below
the sands are loose, and beyond the river there are meadows as far as the eye can see...

And so that a million hives would be placed in these meadows, sow sweet
herbs, plant honey trees, and let the honey fat flow
glass tubes!.. Enough for how many people!.. Everything is available
to a person, & someone prevents him from doing, some force makes him empty
meadows Apart from bitter herbs, there is nothing to take; honey is wasted.
lie down. ..

Ivan stroked his red mustache, lit a cigarette and laughed: it was ridiculous
good, but the good is lost... A bucket rolled down the hill and froze

scrambled over the pebbles. Ivan looked around - the girls’ skirts were rustling from the wind,
shimmer.

p.

“The moonlight evenings in Vedrin are beautiful, they are conducive to romance.”

This is how telegraph operator Pyotr Petrovich once put it, a man
30 years old, eternal bachelor and nanny, very fond of the word “intelligence”
Ligence."

Pyotr Petrovich called himself an anarcho-communist and was very
asked: what party does the school teacher belong to? And when-
`came to the conclusion: the school teacher belongs to the party of 9e6-ers,
because he is not indifferent to land policy and the Kli wears a beard.
now, and complacency is written on his face. Him, Pyotr Petrovich,
his face is wrinkled, with a black mustache, and he doesn’t need anything except

BASIC PREREQUISITE.

Any social movement has its source of interest
sy of one class or another.

It may currently be significant in its size.
mahu, the depth of penetration into the depths of the class, rich in its own way ©0-
holding, can only be faintly outlined and be in the initial phase
initial accumulation of one's values - one way or another, it is always
its roots go into the industrial subsoil.

1 Position. this is entirely applicable to proletarian culture,
arose in the proletariat and in it has its social
class base.

When studying it, it is necessary to highlight as a general basis—
the technique of machine capitalism, which forms the elements of the proletariatments of the new culture, and then a number of other “special moments”,
contributing to its further growth.

Let us single out from the concept of “proletarian culture” one of the essential
its main features: the spirit of comradely cooperation.

We will therefore assume that all processes that expand the field
such cooperation, strengthening the mutual connection between its s5-
participants, contribute to the formation of a new culture in
proletariat. In this case, the development of the elements of proletarian culture
tours not only as a principle or theoretical construction, & not
mediocre in the practice of life itself, will be relatively quantitative
the effective growth of the proletariat, the extent of mutual dependence of individual
its different units from each other and, in general, to an increasing importance
in the social process of production. These moments, in turn,
conditioned by the machine technology of capitalism and arising from
her forms of economic organization.

The decisive moment of the emergence and further growth of a new
“machine culture” in the proletariat is new technology; task
comes down to a possibly condensed presentation of the most important points of its
development and especially to the history of tools.

A typical production tool for modern industry
is a machine, or more precisely; machine system. Machines are “everlasting companions”
kicks of the newest industrial proletarian. She—matshina—played
played the role of a technical center around which per-
senior detachments of the proletariat; she raised his first generations and
laid the foundation for a new social type... |

A complete picture of the relative growth of the proletariat and machines -
new technology would have worked if it had not been possible to comprehensively describe the compactness
all industries ‚ For our purposes this is not unconditional
necessary, and we can limit ourselves to the most important moments. Restored
We see in basic terms the evolution of ‘machines - tools, malgin - engines
and methods for using critical raw materials.

We had to dwell in a little more detail on the machine-
structure because in the general industrial system it is
common power and technological foundation. Growth and development
machine industry and, in particular, machine engineering—
is a constant indicator of the increasing participation of the proletariat

The development of mechanical engineering was directly dependent on
new methods of metal smelting.

Briefly summarized, the most important development points are:

The first blast furnace for smelting cast iron was built in
Rhine Province back in 1443

The use of hydraulic force for blowers gave
technical basis for obtaining high temperatures, and thereby
cast metal. Zugong smelting from Germany was then transferred
to England, and in 1619. Dod Dudley used the military to...
melting cast iron is not charcoal, but coal. Ego emergency
importance of the invention, however, was not further developed and
revived again through the efforts of Abraham Derby (1709).

The final replacement of charcoal with coke should be timed
by 1735

A significant step forward in the development of iron smelting
associated with secondary smelting of cast iron in cupola furnaces, which organizationally
led, among other things, to a peculiar separation of foundries from
blast furnaces and establishing a closer connection between the former and machine-
construction factories.
No. 9 CULTURAL ISSUES. 87

It is then necessary to note the discovery of new methods of obtaining
iron: puddling—invention of the Englishman Cort in 1784;
then - bessemerization (1855), which makes it possible to obtain in 15-20 minutes
high quality cast steel; then - application of the Siemens method.
Martev, and—one of the latest achievements: invention by the British
Thomas and Gilchrist memethod of processing cast iron containing even
large quantities of phosphorus (1878).

Directly dependent on metal smelting, the production process also developed.
coal industry, and even, in connection with the growth of steam

|, MASS PRODUCTION.

Another technical factor of the new cultural structure is:

in large quantities, from a practical point of view it is quite onerelatives,

U. THE DISCOVERY OF THE BOURGEOISIE.

Turning now to mocops that are rooted in the conditions
the lives of other classes hostile to the proletariat.

The main and decisive point is the general crisis of the organiza-
nizatory functions of the former ruling classes.

Great social storms of the past—bourgeois revolutions—
liberated, unleashed in due time the ‘creative initiative of the
of the new class that came to the Lord.

The accumulation of wealth in individual hands, slowly occurring
during the era of feudalism. received a significant boost due to the opening of new
countries, especially America, with the presence of sea routes to Ivdia, you
a cartload of new colonies of precious metals and stones, mercilessly
significant robbery of the native population, trade and exploitation of slaves.
If we were to add here the various methods used at home
in the metropolis, at one time recorded by Marx under the name
concept of “primitive accumulation”—as the expropriation of lands from
rural population and churches, then the prerequisites will become obvious
industrial capitalism.
No. 9 CULTURAL ISSUES. 47

But, besides “capital”, i.e. labor crystallized in the past
and which is a tool for the exploitation of living labor in the present,

technical, commercial, administrative tasks together, it is necessary
be able to put the enterprise into motion, manage it, be oriented
knowledgeable in the market, to capture economic and, often, political
conjuncture, etc.—and the larger the event, the greater the number
number of factors have to be taken into account and in a correspondingly greater
scale to develop organizational skills. And the field of activity
For industrial capitalism, the unimaginable was opening up. Demand
grew stronger in the domestic market; the distant external market beckoned high
profits, stimulated the growth of industry, developed
The organizer of the bourgeoisie is a genius. Capitalists, if not themselves
were inventors, came out with the latter to the company and ©0-
not only did they organize together. but also led the factories
acceptance (chapr., Watt and B plantOlton in Sogo, near Birmingham).

technological techniques—Nasmith, Seller, Whitworth, Dod Dudley,
Wilkinson and others. They also transferred technical achievements to other
ge countries. One can note the activities of two Englishmen, Moby and
Wilson, who after the Napoleonic Wars and the conclusion of peace or-
organized a model plant in Charenton, near Paris (in 1822)
and thus gave impetus to the development of French mechanical engineering and cast iron
smelting business. They willingly entered into agreements with the French
capitalists, organized factories at their expense, put them into operation,
technically supervised them for a certain period of time, in a word—
carried out for the first time the functions of technical consultation in a broad
scale. ‚ at

M. WORLD WAR.

The next peculiar moment in a number of factors promoting
The process of self-isolation of the working class is a world war.

The last war, more than any other, bore
features characteristic of modern technology and economics: world
scale, mass production of destruction, rapid pace
development and machine forms of its manifestation.

If we ignore the subjective human material, then it is important
The greatest weapon of war was modern technology: tanks and guns,
airplanes and submarines, poisonous gases and electric current,
as weapons of destruction; railways and cars, field tech-
legraph and telephone as communication tools, etc.

On the quantitative side, the main cadre of the armies is most likely
recruited from the peasantry; for agricultural countries this is out of bounds
doubts'), but the main frame on which the technology of war rested—
this is the industrial proletariat. The true heroes of the war are: artillery
lerist, pilot and sailor, driver and telegraph operator, mechanic and fitter, technician
nick and chemist. The war rested on the proletariat, just as it rested on it.
all production continues. General’ “ideological-political” ru-
the captaincy was, of course, in the hands of the state—this apparatus
bourgeoisie, which enjoyed the highest command headquarters of its
armies as an instrument of their political, and ultimately eco-
ical, tasks. But the actual organizer of the war was the highest
technical and administrative intelligentsia, and direct
the leader of the technology of war was the proletariat, and, first of all,
Firstly, its qualified layers.

If the statement is correct that the winner in the Franco-Russian
war there was a German teacher who gave a higher level of
sticism, flexibility in the psyche of an ordinary German soldier, which made
his more initiative, not getting lost in an unexpectedly new situation
new, able to quickly and accurately find the correct reaction to
her, then no less a hero of the world war was the “master”, “technical
technical director of a machine-building plant.

What did the war give to the proletariat? The immediate death of the famous
of its personnel, decreased performance, deskilling,
lack of a healthy production atmosphere in the initial period
working life for young people called up for arms is innumerable
mental trauma, not to mention the greatest disintegration of production
active forces during the war, with all that follows for
proletariat consequences. But what especially needs to be emphasized is
this deep and growing distrust of the organization
to the torical genius of the bourgeoisie.. This was reflected with particular sharpness in

questions. Let's take the article © Party policy of the Russian Communist Party in art. m

of proletarian poets and so-called fellow travelers). Politics

tive us politically. *

TO THE ART OF THE WORD.
1. COMMONLY KNOWN AS APPLIED TO POETIC FORM.
(In search order). `

Our topic should begin with well-known provisions.

What is poetic form?

It is distinguished from prosaic speech by: rhythmic structure, sound
figurativeness and special musical division of the entire poetic
works, and these parts are like musical phrases -
walk in some mysterious correspondence with both rhythm and internal
the early flow of an unspeakable theme.

- A thought expressed is a lie, - in a chant and racing manner (still
far from Tyutchev) poets justified their inclination to write poetry.

Why!

After all, we cannot remain silent like this. We must express our...
And here a small change took place, noticeable, perhaps, only
for a sober person: instead of thought, feeling was substituted.

But it is possible to express an idea, I wrote about this beautifully in my
timeI am still Potebnya: only with a word does a thought begin, and the word with it
controls, and every dog, mosquito and in general has what it takes to say a word
animal, to say the least.

Why strive and yearn for something that does not exist?

And even worse: why call it “no” impudently and hypocritically?
the ringing name of “thought”?

To know through experience, mystical contemplation, the so-called
by intuition, a supersensibly specific ability of the priest,
mental patient and bourgeois artist...

...But we'd be going too far if we continued
this thought of ours.

Listen!

After all, if the stars

Light up - 2
So does anyone need this?
This means it is necessary
So that every evening

Fuck the roofs
Did at least one star light up?

Not only pre-revolutionary Mayakovsky, but also all previous
poets directed their ardent desire to “know” nowhere else
place like this one:

- Why light up the stars? >

Genuine thought would in this case ask not “why”, but “why?”
“what” and, probably, would be able to answer herself as best she could, using the given

knowledge of astrophysics and astronomy.
But no, it is absolutely necessary:

- Why do the stars light up?
Then thought turns away contemptuously, taking away from the poet

instruments of its logical verbal expression, and the latter remains
face to face with my inexpressible hole,

paaiya, E oO OE E

90 UAH. No. 9

The result is not prosaic speech, but what we re-
numbered higher: rhythmic structure, sound visualization, musical
cal phrases, mysterious correspondences, an inexpressible theme, in a word -
poem.

It looks like the poet is constructing an intricate ritual
a motor system to lift... a blade of grass from the ground. ^

What’s easier: pick it up, touch it, name it and assign it
ready to eat!

Thus dictates thought, which has never lost its inherent
meanings somewhere to apply on things.

But experience is a completely different matter...

Thus, barely approaching the poem and still avoiding
any conclusions, we feel that we are immediately losing our solid
and solid ground andimmersed in a mystery, in a ritual, in something very
similar to religion.

In the previous paragraph it was not by chance that we mentioned religion
gyu, talking about the poem.

Their similarity is far from accidental.

Religion in a broad sense is characterized as a comprehensive
supersensible explanation of the world. This is its original quality,
replacing scientific, positive, materialistic knowledge of things.

And here we have before us a thought that is far from new: a poem, which
no matter how small it is, at least “gradioza about a matchbox”
(I. Severyanin) - always strives to be the answer to everything.

It will not agree to anything less.

Many smart and subtle people wrote about this at one time.
teachers of poetry, at least our Belinsky.

But - 1

and we will not need sources.

Take any poem by Anacreon, Lermontov, Byron,
Verhaeren, Blok, Mayakovsky - an irrefutable fact will confront
through your eyes: depicting a certain vicious circle of reality
ity, the poet deduces into the universe, as if projects it into something,
what is currently absorbing him: the labo of the rose and the nightingale, or
to a beautiful “stranger”, or to a “riot stamping”, etc.

The poet’s “echo” is not only that he responds to some
phenomenon, but also in the fact that, responding to it, he strives to respond to
all the voices he had ever heard that were absorbed into him
and constituted its nature.

It is not without reason that one can judge the appearance of a poet from one poem.
One poem is already a small worldview, while art
nature-synthesizing power.

But, we repeat, all these are old truths. And therefore we will not
it takes them a long time to stop.

It is only characteristic that this “answer to everything” becomes
the more lyrical the poem, the closer it is to the immediate
new experience, to the sacrament.

Organic kinship of a poem with religion with even more
law can be asserted based on the historical origin
Research Institute of Poetry.

Here again, the most general references will suffice. Still We-
Selovsky researched that poetry came from a certainprimitive
No. 9 art 91

syncretism of music, dance and words, which was nothing more than
namely a cult. :
“And Miriam” the prophetess, Aaron’s sister, took a tympanum in her hand
and all the women followed her with timbrels and rejoicing. And she sang
Miriam before them: “Sing to the Lord, for he is highly glorified.”

But this is a later, biblical syncretism. In its pure
form, it goes back to much more hoary times: people in animal
skins gathered around the fires and danced to a simple muse -
ku, singing the divine motif in recitative...

The same phenomenon includes the Dionysian festivals with goats
by some artists in Greece, who for the first time outlined, on the one hand—
‘a lyrical dithyramb, in another a tragedy. }

But you can read about all of this in its proper place.

The main thing is important for us: the remnants of syncretism and religious
essence accompany poetry throughout its entire existence
vaniya. right up to the present day,

Let us mention only the so-called jugglers of the early Middle Ages.
kovya, who performed Swap$01з 4е it and the lives of the saints to the accompaniment
ment viola - dancers and singers at the same time; in Rus' they are
at one time the storytellers of the various “Pigeon Books” corresponded
and epics...

In modern times, opera can serve as an example of syncretism.

tours, religion in poetry, as a direct plot and cult,
gradually disappears, but, having lost its cult significance in the plot,

if not for the same purpose as the primitive cult participant—

- as if with a uniform beating of the heart, humbly or enthusiastically
having sincerely humbled your sinful thoughts, responded to the essence
with his own strength, no, not knowledge, but against incomprehensible forces...

The poet is ready to do anything to avoid thought and logic, so that
in his response to be bestial and simple, like a moo:

this is how the sea responds to the moon at night, and this is how the dog
she howls, struck by sad memories
about yourNeolithic age...

lyrics immediately take its place.

new explanation of the world. .

When they have reasons to sing,

With the appearance of Acmeism in the poetic arena (1910-12)
There have been debates about the intensive and entensive meaning of artistic
words. Intensity—a self-sufficient meaning—was held to by symbolic
sheets; the extensiveness of the word—its aspiration to forms of action
telnosti - was supported by young Acmeists.

This is how the reaction in poetry began - even then, before the revolution -
against the isolation of the poetic word from the material thing.

In prose—intensity and extensiveness ‘corresponds to static
versatility and dynamism of the word,

intuitive knowledge, in revultal - static, impressionism,
lyricism

SYMPHONY OF HOOMS.

When the morning whistles blare
for workersainah, -
This is not a call of bondage at all:
this is the song of the future.
A. Gastev.

Of all the arts, music has the greatest social and organizational
lowering power.

The most ancient myths testify to the awareness of this power of the human
humanity since time immemorial.

Orpheus tames wild animals with music.

Joshua crushes the strongholds of Jericho with trumpets.

Amphion, with the sounds of the lyre, erects majestic temples from the rocks:
stone colossi form by themselves to his music.

Pythagoras hears the “harmony of the spheres” in the cosmic mechanism itself.
Nick, the movement of heavenly bodies. ‘`

From myth to history: music and mass song are inevitable at-
tributes to the social life of humanity in the most solemn
her moments; festivals, religious and everyday rituals, collective
Long labor (from barge hauler to soldier) is unthinkable without songs and music.

High organization of the collective factory and art
hard work in a capitalist society, it would seem, should
was to create a worthy Form of musical embodiment... however,
October was needed to give life to the idea of a “beep symphony!”:
anarchic tendencies in the production system itself and fear of
uniting producers, workers - did not allow it to be real
registration The morning chaotic roar was still “the call of the un-
will“...

The revolution has come. One night—an unforgettable night!—a thousand-
Red Peter roared in a loud chorus of beeps and sirens, and in response
Hundreds of trucks rushed to the outposts in the back alleys of the outskirts,
rifles bristling with bayonets... The Red Guard flew towards
I’ll cut Kornilov’s avguards... As I wanted, as it was necessary
at this terrible moment to bind the roaring chaos with a single will and replace
give anxiety the victorious anthem of the International!

Great October. The beeps are blaring all over Russia again,
tools... and there is still no single organizing will.

19th year. Volga. Lower. We escort the trains towards Col-
chaku to Kazan. We roar goodbye with the whole squadron until it disappears
There's a gray haze coming out of our eyes... we're finally making our first attempt at organizing...
It’s difficult, it’s not possible,too many sirens, but still array outlines
The International can be distinguished...

22nd year. Baku. Opening navigation. 26 oil fleet vessels from
go to ‘Astrakhan’. The entire fleet, docks, factories roar... A grandiose orchestra
ny. It was decided: on the 5th anniversary of October it will sound harmonious. And he
sounded.

We want. so that on the 6th anniversary every city that has de-
dozens of steam boilers, organized a worthy “accompaniment” Ok-

celebration of the year, and we give here instructions for organizing the “sym-
phonies of beeps" in relation to various local conditions.

After successful experience, this is no longer difficult: all you need is initiation.
tiva and energy.

MAGI STRAL. ^

One of the most important conditions for successful execution is
preliminary construction of a steam boom line.

The main line is installed either at a convenient location
in a factory boiler, or on a steam locomotive or steamboat (in Vaku there was

y E
eee

installed on the destroyer Dostoyny). Advantages of mobile
the main lines are obvious: at various moments of the celebration it can be
served at one point or another in the city and even demonstrated
independently in the surrounding area.

The construction of the main line is very simple: screw onto a common pipe
there are from 20 to 50 beeps (mostly cylindrical: their
easier to rebuild). The pipe is given one shape or another, depending on
versatility from the installation site: straight, semicircular, two-three-arm,
indifferent - from a sound point of view. It is only important that the supply
the pair was in the center, and drain taps were installed at the ends
or valves to drain the water before performing, otherwise the water will
ejected through the beep valve and the rhythmic precision of the

. niya ‘is lost. The beeps are adjusted by shortening the
stuffy column in a retractable cylinder in any way: piston,
or simply by hammering a wooden block on top and then
fixing it at a given depth. The tree must be chosen
it is hygroscopic, otherwise it will swell under the influence of steam outside- |
accuracy of adjustment is achieved after 2-3 restartspetitions. Stacked beeps.
are very weakly adjustable (only within one tone, ea-`
my major is thirds) by backing the washers and therefore removing
reduction of the lower circumference of the glass from the steam jet: significant
changing the pitch will be to the detriment of timbre and tone strength. If you are needed -
rich tones, which the existing beeps do not provide, can be created by

#9 INVENTION AND CRAFTMANSHIP. 111

window in a cylindrical horn or eccentric installation
kana to achieve overtone sound (octave, fifth and double
an octave higher). However, with such
beeps require caution and
multiple checks, they can-

; hesitation at the slightest change

steam pressure.

squeeze it, as if tuning,

Number of tones: minimal (for the full melody of the International
nala) 12: e, {, iz, v, #13; z, v, s,, 9, ©, &, v. It is advisable to add

INDIVIDUAL HONES,

You can bypass the highway only if there is sufficient co-number of movable boilers (steam locomotives and ships) and the possibility of their
concentration in one area (station, railway pier).

But even in this case, the highway, as a kind of “musical
instrument,” greatly contributes to the integrity of the impression.

With a large number of stationary beeps (factories, factories,
steam mills, docks, depots, etc.) they can be used in groups
Pami in the development of the musical picture. For example, in Baku such a
at once (see “Order” in the appendix) a musical car-
a mud of anxiety and battle. Signals for groups to perform beyond the range
distances are served by gun salvos. Groups are configured
in compact harmonies and provide the background for the central collective and ma-

gistrals. It is necessary to take into account the sound distances from the signal
guns to the group and from the ‘group to the celebration area, so that
the entry of the groups was timely. Performed by the International
distant groups do not participate, since the cannon is already playing at this time
the role of a “big drum” and cannot signal at a distance.

The moving highway may be temporarily delayed for
strengthening of this or that group, but there should be a government response to the fan
Puppy in its place.

SIRENS, VEHICLES, BELLS, AZRO.

Sirens of the fleet and factories constitute a special group of instruments,
not involved in the harmonic development of a musical work
nia, They perform independently, in special episodes, alone
or chords (in parallel and in counter-movement) on an organ point -
those bass ones. whistle under rifle and machine-gun salvoes, mainly
zom, as a means of sound recording and signaling. With good performance
threads." you can, of course, try to give them both harmonic and
even youthful tasks, this is already a virtuoso element, are not easy
introduced into the design of ordinary tonal music. „Differential
This “music of siren sounds is entirely in terms of the future. Today
we are barely groping for the laws of its specific harmony and
melodies. AB

Vehicles located in close proximity
to the place of celebration (inone of the adjacent streets), valuable, main
in a different way, with its noise effects, but with a sufficient amount
quality of tone signals can create a special timbre-harmony
group. The noise of the engines themselves (especially trucks), as well as
low-flying air and seaplanes create amazing effects
amazing emotional action.

The ringing of bells, wabati, funeral and jubilantly joyful -—
are applied in the relevant episodes - without taking into account the harmonic
concept, or the structure of the symphony is chosen in advance using
in relation to the available bells (rhythmic change-
the ringing of naval “flasks” in Baku accompanied the entire execution of In-
ternational). :z

ARTILLERY.

If there are scattered beeps over a large area, it is necessary to have
for signaling, at least one, heavy weapon and the ability to hit
from it with a live projectile (shrapnel is not suitable, because, exploding
in the air, is the most dangerous and produces a second explosion sound that can knock down
confusing the performers). The “big drum” can also give field
weapon. - y

Experienced bully shooters (again, subject to live fire
tape) not only imitate a drum roll, but also beat out complex
new rhythmic figures. Idle rifle salvoes and frequent firing
packs are good for sound writing moments.

TOWER,

To conduct a symphony in close proximity
A tower is erected near the execution center on an elevated place.

The simplest device is a pair of telegraphs connected at the ends
60 pillars with a Swedish mast. At the top there is a platform with a barrier.
#9 INVENTION AND CRAFTMANSHIP. 113

same =

On the side there are sockets for flag poles, or a rope accessory
tion to jerk them up. The tower must be designed for the beam
view of the performers in the clear sky. The colors of the flags are selected. most
sharper (marine signaling), visible well from afar. Navy,
locomotives, battery, machine gunners, vehicles - take positions
close to the tower to see the signals directly. To the tower
a field telephone must be connected to its station, connected
c bbattery, celebration area, training ground and the most important groups
Pami, It’s useful to have a strong mouthpiece and human (live) connection
with the highway. Conducting (metric)—right hand; left -
artillery and other signals are emitted. Battery - per hundred
another closer to the celebration square than the tower, in order to avoid
late shot.

NOTES.

The attached sample text notes of the International gives pre-
knowledge about the type of notes in general. Rhythmics are written on one line
figures are printed in this form and then emphasized from
hands of “parts” of individual tones,

With such notes you can not only perform, but also rehearse
symphony indoors. Just give it to the performers
corresponding externally small sounding devices that produce only

8
114 V A ’ No. 9

and

one tone (for example, copper voices from a harmonium, clay and tin-
new children's whistles, etc.).

It must be borne in mind that on the highway each performer
The body has two tones - for the left and right hands. Party of each:
the hand should be underlined with a different color of ink. a

Accordingly, at the rehearsal, the main line workers need to be given
two whistles. It doesn’t matter if the entire symphony at rehearsals is sound
start on whistles an octave higher.

The smallest divisions allowed for performance are eighths,
at the tempo of the International, subject to conducting at 3 beats.
Smaller rhythmic beats are not achieved with sufficient clarity.

EDITION OF THE SLOGAN.

(To the assignment of the CE Pfroletkult for the October celebrations).

Our time has turned the previous narrow political agitation
purely intellectual influence into a complex system of pressures on
psyche of the masses. Expressive qualities of all phenomena and events, voeh’
things and human actions are organized in the direction that
the impression they evoked contributed to the class's treasury
combat effectiveness. Emphasized mistakes of the enemy, organizational s06-
significant improvements, education of emotions - hatred, on the one hand
rona, comradely solidarity, < another - that’s one thousandth
of the whole process, the huge process of agitation, which inevitably
accompanies the process of revolution.

An agitator is a promoter, a director of emotions. Propaganda - all kinds
thing that is intended to attract intense attention to something
or another phenomenon, push the desired action, increasing the mental

ical pressure of people, providing the action with the right amount
emotional gunpowder.

The word is a qualified tool of agitation. In the spontaneous pro-
in the process of developing public sentiment, it is usually the phenomenon that
and words that excite the psyche arise spontaneously, involuntarily.
Maybe the cry of a whooper is the most powerful way to collect
or discharge emotional energy. An indistinct cry in which
more throat spasms than meaningful words, often shifts
mountains and breaks concrete walls. This happens when quantitative
new accumulation of emotion has occurredb, and she just needs a push, she needs

just to... nerves trembled and quantity turned into quality
actions.

But when the process of formation of the social psyche ceases
be carried out in explosions, and a properly organized attack begins
the development of this emotional flow, controlling its level, dis-
just a few times to direct it in the right direction—to replace the unorganized
The organized word appears in front of the natural, spontaneous word.

Its expressive qualities should:. be taken into account and weighed;
the building of speech must be built based on knowledge of the material,
taking into account the task and accurately understanding the properties of the team to which
to whom the word is addressed.

Here the word should not be born, not spewed out with inspiration,
a— be done.

Our time is before the workers who do agitation with words,
poses the responsible task of processing the slogan.

The processed slogan becomes a kind of canonical
literary form, similar to the way in everyday life of the 18th and early 19th centuries
There was an epigram (later extinct).
118 HP; No. 9

At the beginning of the 19th century in Germany, Nazirite moralists cultivated
moral and religious maxim (such maxims written in
glass boards, found in every Lutheran family). In the middle
centuries - mottos and advertising aphorisms of guild craftsmen. Finally,
in oral folk literature we have a similar form of polo-
Vits, and in factory-town life - a ditty stanza.

All the above! shapes can be used in a slogan.
We can build a slogan like an epigram and epitaph - ridiculing
enemy. We must necessarily maintain the nature of the order in it -
telial maxims and proverbs.

And at the same time, we must maintain in the slogan: 1) precise
its correspondence with the theme, 2) visual (rather than sound) character
its and 3) instantaneous action.

Thematic precision is as difficult as, say, composition.
A telegram on a complex issue must be written in 10 words.

’” The topic must be exhausted, and at the same time the writing technique—
rhythm, consonance, images, syntax—very narrow the field whenchanges
any words and combinations. To present the essence of the matter to those limited
set of phrases that is available to “verbal affairs”
master" is one of the most difficult tasks, and he learns this succinctly
ical aphorism').

The pictorial character is that the slogan reads
eyes, not ears. His words and their cementing must speak
speak for themselves, they cannot be supported either by voice modulation or declarative
with a gesture. The place of the slogan is on the board, pediment, name,
lot. Here is its relationship with an epitaph, a motto, a sign.

The instantaneous action of a slogan makes the methods of processing it similar.
with the techniques of advertising and newspaper headlines. In contrast to the maxim,
hanging on the wall of the room, and a permanent sign - a slogan used
on the day of a festival, demonstration, often promoted by
street on the canvas - must be stuck in consciousness after a glimpse
glance. It should be built in such a way that it will be chained to the fleeting
pay attention to yourself, at least for a second, and then ingrain into consciousness for
perhaps for a long time. It should be like a burdock, I grab-
Even if someone accidentally hits him, the tail will whine.

The first duty is to call the eyes to you (the moment is typically rec-.
lame)—usually served not by its sententious side, but by its middle-
image properties: board, paint, font, line arrangement. But,
the second part - to be remembered, to cling to the memory - must give
zung, as a purely speech construction. That slogan is worthless, remembering
which, they draw out the location of the lines with their hands, but cannot remember
thread of not a single word, at best the rhythm booms, but even without con-
standing to say what the slogan is about—Curzon or the tax in kind.

INVENTION IN THE POSTER.

The poster is a product of the capitalist era.

Although the first posters appeared in the form of posters from Parisian theaters
atrov-zucchini, but the bourgeoisie quickly took advantage and assimilated everything
expressive means of a poster for the purposes of commercial competition
tions.

The poster is born of struggle.

The struggle in the market, the struggle on the fronts:political, military,
ideological. The poster begins to live 060bo intensely in acute
moments of struggle. Aggravation of the commodity crisis, election campaign
into parliaments, war, revolution—they push motley colors onto the streets of cities,
big-eyed, loud-mouthed army of posters.

The brainchild of struggle, the poster is dynamic.

Dynamic in its ideology, formal structure, conditions
production and social role. The dynamism of the poster makes it
specifically inventive art.

Poster is the most expressive form of industrial invention.
craftsmanship and craftsmanship. |

`As a production product (and mass production), pla-
kat does not (and should not have) any once and for all fixed
bathroom shape.

The form of the poster is new every time.

It does not arise as a result, but is produced in every new
case and rosetog!. It is the result of three conditions:

1) Purpose of the poster (social-teleological moment);

2) Technical resources, material, visual aids
etc. (production moment);

3) Conditions of perception by the environment and conditions of influence on it
(social and psychological moment).

Reflecting on poster art, one cannot talk about impression
Zionist, expressionist, constructive, etc. posters.
For “naked”, abstractly, is the conceivable form of a poster, in which
it was possible to “pour in” any content - it cannot be.

How does the process of inventing the form of a poster proceed (when
the master is consciously aware of all stages
of his work), or how it should proceed (when the required consciousness
The master doesn’t know how to show skill)?

To answer such a question, you need to make an orientation
to an artist - an easel painter, and to an engineer - a production worker. By-
build and evaluate the shape of a poster as a mass-produced product
production, perhaps by comparing it with the most typical factories
there is mass industry. Almost every manufactured product produced at
The market is a tool or means for a specific purpose.
Every tool or medium is an object withcial,
not having a self-sufficient existence.

63
No. GB mo

Socio-economic and formal production content
The fabrication of mass industry is determined by the purpose of the thing.

The shape of such a thing is dictated by its purpose and material. She
must be expedient and utilitarian. Purpose of the subject of study
defines the scope of its social distribution. Example: heel,
by varying colors and patterns, takes into account the social composition of consumers
and destinations. :

Consequently, an engineer designing a thing of Mays
bleating means:

1} The purpose of the thing, its consumer function;

2) The scope of its social distribution;

3) Material to be processed; at

4) Technical resources that can be available during production
things.
These four points in turn influence;

a) the labor value of the product, i.e. to normal or average
it is the amount of labor that, given social, economic
technical and technical conditions required for production
point;

Ch 6) consumer value of the product or its social value
useful for consumption.

The exchange value of the product cannot be of interest here,
because the posters are not on sale.

The role of a poster artist is fully adequate to the role of a mechanical engineer.
constructor. Both of them are inventors of the form of a thing, the form is not
self-sufficient, but conditioned by the purpose of the product. Sledova-
It is advisable that when starting to design the poster form, the master should
take into account all the above conditions. And only as a result of this
accounting; a unique poster shape can be created for each
this case, and only for this particular case, So, pro-
production position that the poster master will occupy is truly
Having understood its role, it follows from the very essence of the production of this
kind of manufactured goods.

The master manufacturer, having received an order for a poster, when inventing
regarding its form, will take into account:

1. The consumer function of the poster, its purpose
a one-time, maximum-strong and short blow to the psyche of the visualbody In musical terminology there is an expression asso@p]adiv that
means an even, simultaneous strike of all notes of a chord. Poster
the form similarly concentrates the maxi-
mum of expressiveness ‚The consumer function of the poster due to this
impact differs from the functions of things of mass consumption res-
such a predominance of the psychological element over the material.
A large industry in the development of forms for consumer goods
Niya strives to standardize these forms (electrical fittings,
telephone sets, etc.). This unification of forms achieves
the ease of replacing one thing that has become unusable with another,
similar to it, and the methods of producing items are also normalized,
consumed in large quantities. On the contrary, the poster master, teaching
tying its impact task, its maximum impact on the psyche
viewer by creating the most visually striking expression—
forced to strive not for the standard but for originality.

The unified form, which quickly became familiar to the viewer,
stops making an impact on him, goes unnoticed,
That is the poster loses its dare to be conscripted.

CLUB IN LIFE.

(From the work “On the Guides of the New Life”).

Among the important creative moments of social life
The club needs to be noted.

Give up the habit of living outside of work at the factory, your deputy
whipped family life, only on holidays allowing oneself to socialize
communication with other comrades; love the camaraderie
in the club; live in the interests of the entire club team; be satisfied
precisely that grain of creative work that you put into the total
the matter itself—this is already a big psychological shift from the meager replacement
the harshness of family life.

The first thing that educates a visitor is the atmosphere of the club.

The houses are stuffy, the smell of burnt onions, there are icons in the corners (although
often and “without use”), two or three tattered books on the table,
sometimes a cheap gramophone © ugly trumpet and sharp screaming
mi sounds. On the wall, next to some young couple under
pen“—Marx (concession to the spirit of the times).

taste, development and needs. Music.

0 MASS WORK OF THE CLUB.

Recently, among cultural workers there has been a lot of debate about the predominance of
advantages of this or that method in club work: some will give
above all lectures, others see a panacea for all the evils of club life
in the eco-cursion method, others put forward the slogan of political-enlightenment
positive education through artistic work (agitation trials, incest
decorations, posters), etc.

At the same time, the content of the club’s
work. Pletnev’s book “Workers’ Club” provides an analysis of the content
all branches of club work (economics, politics, everyday life, professional movement)
zheniya, etc.), and from the content of each. questions raised
those shock moments, the coverage of which is absolutely necessary in
club work. |

Both the methods and the content of the work were not invented by theorists,
they only realized and illuminated the trends that we have in
club life, in that very club practice, where, depressed, everyone
variety of content and methods, helplessly flounder
blowing in clubs. That “reassessment of values” of club work, which
is now in all cultural institutions, and those instructions for practice,
which stem from it are of very great importance for the club
workers, but, nevertheless, they cannotbring to life
most of the good instructions, due to the inability to place
in time, club material and the impossibility for them to measure.
separate parts of the work. In fact, unions argue that
the most important work of clubs is in the field of trade union movement, district committees
they base party work among the masses on clubs, and organize political education
educational work is in the center, then there are issues of everyday life, ideology
it. d.

And all these questions really are part of the essence of the club
work. But how can I group my work so that everyone doesn’t suffer?
these individual types of it, how to use one or another method of it, from
which everyone in different conditions can give both positive and
negative aspects - these are the questions that interest club members
practitioners along with (and often stronger than) issues of general club
politics.

If we take a closer look at the club work as it is going now, it
will seem to us sewn from separate pieces, like those blankets from
multi-colored shreds that the bourgeois women in the province loved so much.
Let’s take the mass work schedule of a well-functioning club:

Tuesday—lecture on natural science.

Friday—lecture on the trade union movement.

Sunday morning—excursion to the radio station,

Sunday evening—the play “Paris”.

Next week:

Tuesday—lecture on aviation.

Friday—lecture on primitive culture.

Sunday morning—excursion to the Tretyakovaya Gallery,

Sunday evening—concert by groups, etc. etc.

"ART AND CLASSES". For 3-4 years in Russian art there has been

In a number of articles that make up this book, Arvatov, using the Marxist method,
house, consistently develops the idea that the form of production art
tion is determined by the entire course of development of economic factors. Specific her
implementation follows from the new economic structure of the social economy
creation, the creator of which is historically called to be. working class. Dialectically
Developing the idea, Arvatov gives a sociological analysis of old forms of art
and in some places makes apt criticism of bourgeois easelth painter
stva. Revealing the genesis of art forms, he in the first article, “Capitalism and art”
“natural construction” provides an analysis of the relationships between “pure” forms
art and handicraft production of guild masters.

In the Middle Ages, in the era of individualistic labor, art
penetrated into industry because “there was no difference in society then
in forms of labor." But when “the capitalist collectivization of production began”
", the artist, remaining "within the limits of the previous individual labor", was
removed from direct participation in the creation of material values.
The methods and forms of mass production technology did not coincide with the methods of art.
hard work. Remaining overboard, the artist isolated himself in his circle
"Spetsovskaya" region. The artist first moved on to “making luxury goods”,
and then began to deal only with “selected”, especially “noble” forms
and materials and create only “beautiful” things. So it took shape in the mind
“bourgeois aesthetics” view of the artist as the “creator” of the highest spiritual
values. This is how easel art became established as a form of self-sufficient
in value and a completely independent “picture”. Life, production and art
separated from each other. “You can’t expect practical benefits from art.”
elk, and since the artist no longer felt the organic connection of his
cases with collective construction; he declared art an end in itself, and his
fruits are absolutes.” .

This first article prepares material for ‘that characteristic of easel
painting and sculpture, which is the subject of the second article, “Easel Art.”

Revealing the contradictions of modern easel forms of fine art
art, Arvatov concerns the inevitable crisis that led to a whole
a group of advanced artists to “escape from the machine”. With the decline of capitalist
economic system, the decline of easel painting is inevitable. By changing the “ideological
the “gical content” of the picture of its existence cannot be saved or justified.
StAnkovism is a bourgeois form of artistic production, and already
For this alone, there can be no talk about any proletarian easel art
and speeches. An easel painting, whatever its subject may be, will always be a product
bourgeois art, even if it was made by a proletarian. And because she is easel,
and because she is a painting, her destiny is never to be proletarian. This is the conclusion
to which Arvatov came somewhat straightforwardly.

Third, perhaps the best article: “Aesthetics of easel painting”
contains criticism of the views on art of “bourgeois aesthetics”. These metaphysical
ical views affirm the intrinsic value of a work of art, pleasure
which is characterized by the “disinterest” of the viewer in extracting any
for practical benefits from his “contemplation”. „The advantage of artistic
contemplation lies in freedom from reality, in complete detachment from it.
ity, Arvatov quotes one of the. representatives of this kind of “bourgeois”

B. Arvatov is undoubtedly a sharp and clear worker of Marxist thought
in the field of art, as he has proven himself in a number of magazine articles ("Pe-
Chat and Revolution”, “Lef”, “Gorn”, etc.). The significance of his works has increased even more
becomes possible if we agree with the obvious fact: Plekhanov’s formulas of art,
sharply revolutionary in their time, and now have not lost their true community,
yet they are still ossified in this community of theirs.

community has finally become an amateur stencil: Marxist critics
and theorists (like Fritzsche), having memorized the “base-superstructure”, still have not found
tried nothing better than to “reveal the content,” reducing this disclosure to
links to sociological, historical and cultural, journalistic, everyday and
of any other nature. Historical view of art (literature), in its own right
turn, turned into such a non-methodological review - sociological,
RE <P everyday, depending only on the tastes and profession of the observer.

Arvatov approaches the matter completely differently. Art is first and foremost
construction system.

Thus, in contrast to the old pseudo-criticism, Comrade Arvatov believes
the class nature of art is not in how its heroes live, feel and act,
i.e. not in the “content” of a work of art, but in its very structure.

Only the structure of an artistic “thing”. expresses what the interaction is
art and life in a given social order.

This interaction in the conditions of a capitalist society is dedicated tobook under review “Art and Classes”. We repeat: Arvatov’s thought is different
stands out for the clarity and sharpness of each individual fragment. However, "Art"
"Socialism and classes" is not a scientific analysis, which, from some quarters, might prompt
the severity and novelty of the issue. :

What is the role of the modern artist in production?

Tarabukin is very attentive to this issue and especially not
tends to solve it too straightforwardly.

Tatlin, the first Russian constructivist, went to the factory to make pots and
burners, threw away his easel and counter-reliefs for this, and... let him be a man
whole and impatient, even if he found himself in his new business, but decisions
he did not give the task, because - and this is what Tarabukin points out - he is not fit for an easel artist.
without any historical and technical training, to immediately climb into modern
variable mass and mechanized production.

This is the “tragedy of the transitional time.”

However, all the ways out of the “tragedy”, in addition to its historical solution, are
person: “if in a narrow professional sense the artist still has nothing to say to the engineer”
Nehru, the work of a constructivist takes on a different meaning when one sees in it
laboratory experience on the organization of material, texture elaboration and design

general problems of art and generally less

In this sense, “An Experience in the Theory of Painting” is a somewhat belated attempt.

But, firstly, better late than never, and secondly, a distinct “formality”
“real” theorization of pictorial experience is necessary for understanding the production
new opportunities arising from it.

— The experience of an easel artist-constructivist (transitional era) has already

notices Tarabukin in another place.

happy among other arts. In short, to this day she is still
did not make any difference from the aesthetic-impressionist criticism of “Libra” and “Apollo”, not counting
including several foreign works, and, perhaps, Punin’s monograph on Tatlin.

The use of a non-method, at least in the most general form, like this

and a long overdue task.

It is enough that Tarabukin applied the formal principle and
han in defining such concepts as “form elements of a pictorial work”
“denia”, “color”, “texture”, “composition”, “rhythm”, “plot as an element of form”.

The formulation of these basic concepts of a work of art in:
writing and almost the entire book is devoted, Some objections are raised only by two
general chapters: on the “essence of art” and on the “problem of reality in painting.”

The point, however, is not about the author’s mistakes, but about insufficient elaboration
of expressions, which, however, have a fundamental meaning.

It is absolutely true that “recognizing “mastery” as the main sign of art,
Tarabukin is ready to consider it objective:

“We are well aware of this,” the author writes in the pre-final chapter, “
when we evaluate a Samoan ivory amulet, a tanager figurine
and a bust by Rodin.

And just these examples show that the concept of “mastery” is just as
conclusionincluded in the conditions of the historical, class and other environment, as the concept of “taste”,
“beauty”, etc.

Tarabukin dissociates the “aesthetic vocabulary” from the concept of “skill” and,
however, does not provide a formulation of this difference. On the next page even confused
says: “the concept of mastery is also relative” and finally finds salvation
in the template: “mastery is the organic connectedness of idea and form.”

All this is good and in accordance with the authoritative testimony of all the wreaths, but
the insufficiency of such formulations in the face of revolutionary tasks
art is obvious.

Tarabukin did not define revolutionary skill:

- This is how tanager figurines were made, this is how they should be done. Form de
must match the content!

It’s better not to have any definitions than to be treated to such general and stagnant
mature. .. oranges.

In the last chapter of the book, “the problem of reality in painting,” we find
let us have similar idealistic vagueness:

- At that time; how old art, writes Tarabukin, is characterized
the connection of pictorial forms with the forms of the external real world (community, comrade.

than, for example, Suprematists and non-subject-oriented people who collect colorful

book that new art should create an ‘artistic thing, self-sufficient

“WAVES OF PROLETKULT”. Unfolding Ekaterinoslav’s “Waves”

Ekaterinoslavsky Province. Proletkult. come across something like “children’s handwriting”
1923 on themes about the revolution. It is known, after all, that

“October” in literature (especially poetry)
creative) already has a respectable template for words and a stylistic stamp, and
young people love to imitate the “big ones”, although they often lag behind them... There were
such cases: heroic songs about October were already sung in the center, along the streets
In Moscow the NEP was already on the move, writing work was disappearing into the depths of ideology and
in the accumulation of forces, and there, on the ground, they were just beginning to delay: “October has encircled
cities,”—from belated literary heroism it is not far to philistinism and traffic
reta style. It happened like that.

And so, you deploy “Waves of Proletkult”. Signatures: student Lito Agapov,
student Lito Mikh. Hungry, the student is lit... In a word, both under poetry and under prose—
all the same studio artists, from the first to the last (almost) page of the collection. This is good.

And this “how” turns out to be not at all what you expect (with the general tendency
doubtful and based on past experience).

Let's say briefly: proletarian poetry grows from the ground and is no longer nourished by Moscow-
Russian “Forges”, but in layers of their own black soil, deposited in equal
least in Ekaterinoslav and Yaroslavl.

This is the first remark that the collection “Waves of Proletkult” evokes.

In other words, local revolutionary poetry has ceased to be schoolchildren
from the elders and took the path of organic growth. This is an undoubted shift and stage
development. From the heroic false classicism of "October" local literary
cells are moving towards genuine revolutionary realism. How wide
this development, of course, is still difficult to judge, but realism, organicity and self-
the validity of “Waves of Proletkult” is beyond doubt.

Let's not be unfounded. "Organic"and “independence” in verse
must first of all be expressed formally.

at the “CIRCLE” BOOK DISPLAY.

The Krug publishing house is one of the largest and most active
ny publishing houses in Moscow; it has the ability to collect all the most characteristic
for our time in the field of artistic expression. Editions of "Krug", perhaps
can be considered as a demonstrative exhibition of contemporary art
literature. And, indeed, the Krug publishing house has widely and firmly established
current literary idols. All of them, for the most part, are hunters of modern
ity in its specific manifestations: the events of the revolution, new everyday
layers, pathos of the era.

At the beginning of the activity of private publishing houses, our book market was
filled with poetry; Recently, interest in poetry has greatly decreased; pain-
stability of social life, partial concrete results: revolutionary
great movement—gave rich material for prose writers; publication of collections
poetry has become economically unprofitable.

The Krug publishing house has published relatively few poems throughout its history;
in almanacs very little space is given to poems, and their selection is varied, perhaps
deliberately: along with exquisite exercises in verbal and rhythmic construction
Pasternak's renditions—a somewhat old-fashioned resignation of Ehrenburg and peasant poetry
Oreshina. Kazin and Obradovic round out the variety.

Of the collections of poems, the most significant are N. Aseeva
“Elect”, Kazina “Worker May”, 'N. Tikhonov’s “Braga”, Kazin’s book collects
Most of us are poems already published; poetry—in his usual manner: poetic
zoning of labor processes; everyday incident developed to meaning
space event; a heightened sense of nature and love for things—not
acmeistic contemplative admiration, but effective comprehension,

Aseev's book is explained too thoroughly; somewhat pretentious
the preface warns the reader to ‘followpoetic path
the author from apprenticeship to mastery; carefully outlined in the book itself
the headings carefully assign the appropriate share—to love, to revolutionary feelings—
qualities of the poet, his professional technique, etc.

After Kazin’s life-affirming and socially active poetry in the book
“Working May,” Klychkov’s poems sound like a languid echo of timelessness
"Home songs".

In first place in terms of relative literary significance, perhaps,
plans to stage Malyshkin’s story “The Fall of Dair.” This is a pathetic story
an almost heroic poem about the capture of Perekop. A story without heroes, without individual
Noah. psychology, without a plot, in a word, outside the canon.

The elevated declamatory style of the story does not detract from its storytelling
wealth, and the manner of narrating in the form of alternating contrasting pictures
The tin gives the story special dynamism and compositional unity. Action
unfolds simultaneously from both sides and skillfully brings to the moment
catastrophic resolution. at

In this sense, Malyshkin’s story is compositionally aboutdifferent from the novel
Budantsev’s “Mutiny”, similar in the nature of the material used (also oil-
Soviet movement: first a peasant revolt, then a left-Socialist Revolutionary uprising).
Budantsev either drowned in the material or simply pushed away from it. In the novel
only fragmentary pieces are developed; the rest is a raw interjection: reliable,
sometimes impressive, but more effective in proportion to the significance of the fact itself. Ideologists-
The novel's creative significance is greater than its artistic power, if we use this
conditional division. The fact that Budantsev was the first to bring out the Left Social Revolutionaries should
be, nevertheless, positively noted.

The implementation of the fighting moments of the revolution, the moods of the revolutionary times
menu, the emerging new way of life, the psychology of individual social groups,

maybe negligence, then other authors when coming into contact with these subjects
psychological helplessness, the inability to grasp the true
distinct features and voices of the era, and sometimes the insufficiency of literary means; hence-
yes—often an unconscious distortion, less often a shaded hostile tendency.

howl of life (Pilnyak’s favorite, ever-present themes), in his subsequent collections
he, still in love with antiquity, from there, from the historical gray mossy
stones, spreads to the closest, most topical new thing. Pilnyak—
belated Slavophile; revolution for him is a Russian national riot, rebellion,
Razinovism, the birth of a new Asian culture, in defiance of Europe - comfortable
Noah, prudent, calm hedgehog. The Russian revolution—return
to beloved antiquity, to the seventeenth century, to peasant wisdom; that's why
at Pilnyak the Bolsheviks are new people - Scythians, in largeare illiterate, but
animated by the will to want.

But here’s something completely different—O. Henry, fellow countryman of Taylor, Jack'London and Charlie
Chaplin. However, he is related to every other Yankee with a strong chin,
with a death grip on his fingers, brought up not so much in “culture” as in technology
nik and civilization, speaking in a fashionable way.

This kinship makes Henry no less close and necessary to us than to
the Americans themselves.

He does not bring any “eternal” truths and experiences to us, but to him
you need to take a literary approach: it is necessary, like a strong and healing stream
plot, breaking up the swamp of our psychological prose. :

If he does not already teach the Theosophist from the literature of Andrei Bely, then he will
Pilnyak and his kids can learn from this.

“Stories”, “Soul of Texas”, “Kings and Cabbage” were released back to back
several months, and the time is approaching when the author of these funny and fast
books will catch up with his friend Jack London in the reading community - at the same time
O. Henry is both subtler and more skillful in composition than Jack London—this is also not
must be kept in mind.

If "Stories" are like the cinematography of New York
streets, and “Soul of Texas” is built on a calmer, but firm and cheerful,
treatment of the cowboy plot, then “Kings and Cabbage” is synthetic: here and mathematics
realized will of a civilized American, and the exoticism of a real adventure
Chen's novel, moreover, enclosed in the tropical landscape of South America...

But let us not delude ourselves in advance: of course, O. Henry is not only the son of his
country, but also the son of his society, so he does not even try to overcome the bur-
zhuazny motivation of its plot. His heroes are bankers, brokers, businessmen, traders
govts, clerks, and they do as the dollar tells them. There is no such ideology
assessment, which is made by the plot device of such a bright revolutionary
ner and a fighter like Upton Sinclair.

But reallyThis doesn't make Henry any less interesting.

It is enough that he is far from an apologist for the “free” American de-
mocracy, which ultimately becomes a victim of his cheerful grin.

Describing the strong, fast and tough Yankees, the heroes of the offices and the stock exchange, he
seems to click on their copper foreheads, without, however, taking away any of the American
Kan's merits, without detracting from their “respected position in society,” and, conversely,
Henry approaches tramps, murderers and thugs in a friendly and affectionate manner,
who use mail trains to find many good qualities in them.

The cheerful materialist, energetic and strong-willed Henry becomes here hardly
not whiny, like a kind ‘romantic grandmother’.

But this doesn't suit him.

And, fortunately, this rarely happens to O. Henry.

For us, the literary Henry with his murderous mathematics is much more important.
realistic methods of plot composition.

What are they?

Here, for example, “Kings and Cabbage”: in contrast to the idealistic
motivation of the plot, coming from an “experience” or even a “mystical idea”,
in this novel all the action (plot) is located in terms of a specific struggle
and overcoming the obstacles of reality, the plot is not guided by “experience”.
but calculation and. will.

A natural consequence of this situation are two very important
fact: firstly, there is a movement developing in a continuous plot
action (the psychological plot, if you can call it that, is essentially
tic, it is always something other than a spectacle of subordinate feelings), secondly, the plot
“Kings and Cabbage” unfolds only in material, material forms:
actions, gestures, postures, relationships between things and external positions.

O. Henry is especially characterized by this ascetic neglect of his mother.
alista to the moments of the inner life of her characters, to what they experience;
feel, think. It's their business. What matters to the author and the reader is how they act.

The idealistic prose writer loved the experiences of his heroes, because they
he depicted his contemplation of the world and undergave him sympathetic responsiveness
reader.

As a result, both the prose writer and the reader, like fakirs, buried themselves in the ground (in nir-
vanu of lack of will, of course), instead of digging it up and laying tracts.

But O. Henry prefers action to control it.

An action is the motivation for the plot, and the plot unfolds in actions.

Indeed, in “Kings and Cabbage” the heroes only act (“conversations”

Heroes of the same meaning).

V. FRITCHE. In posing the problem of style

0 STYLE. b:

[ (V. Natapp: eg irgezziutztiz w ЁGerep ip@ Kip$®).
3. ZIMMER. Worldview and forms of style. ("Bulletin of the Socialist
Academy", book 4, M.-P. 1923).

Both of these articles consider the problem of historical-materialistic
explanations of style as a unified system of artistic forms of society. In both
articles of special interest because they were published by academic
mic Marxist body, the methodology of sociological
genesis of styles. But the question of the sociology of styles is holistically posed by
a question about the sociology of artistic form in general—about how a sociologist should
approach the analysis of artistic phenomenava, i.e. about the methodological basis of Marxist
Russian art history. The problem of method is precisely the most controversial and most important
the problem facing Marxism in the science of art—the more carefully
It has to be applied to any performance in this area.

’ Analyzing the views of the German art critic R. Hamann, comrade. Fritsche almost
is entirely adjacent to the analysis of style given by Hamann in his book Oer
Pargez yut sh Geben ia Kipz(".

Namely:

Haman, having given a description of the main properties of pictorial impressionism, asserted
then expects that not only painting is characterized by the corresponding properties
and not only all the art of the era of late capitalism, but “all decisively
we are his cultures. Thus, the style of impressionism, according to Hamann, turns out to be
a general social feature of a certain historical period, rooted
in the technical and economic structure of the latter. Hamann talks about impressionism
in philosophy, morality, exact sciences, etc., and impressionism itself is understood
Hamann toils psychologically, as a special form of thinking and feeling,
worldview and attitude, which grew on the soil of capitalism and determined
methods of creativity in all spheres of culture. For Hamann, therefore, the problem
style is a socio-psychological problem. The same point of view is held by
Comrade is also alive. Fritsche.

It is not difficult to see how such an approach radically distorts the most fundamental
new issues of art history.

Indeed. }

Haman-Fritsche set themselves the task of analyzing styles as a task of formal
but aesthetic, - the solution was on a completely different plane: the authors of the post-
tried to prove that different areas of culture at a given specific moment
give a number of common, similar features. For this there was no need to start from living
The writing and its professional qualities should be compared to philosophy and so on. By-
since all types of superstructures grow on the same basis, insofar as between
they inevitably have similarities and common organizational structures. Search this community
the followingt, starting from the technical structure of society—this is the direct result
waters from the system of historical materialism. If, as Haman and
Fritsche, to take art, even its small volume, as an organizational “standard”
power, and then characterize the entire society as a whole according to such a “standard”, then we
we will have only a superficial analogy, devoid of any scientific
values: worse than that, we will get a methodological aestheticization of culture, dis-
looking at it from the angle of pure art.

With such aestheticization, the question of style is eliminated, the question of general
national typology and is decided for some reason in terms of art. !) Thanks to this

1) It is not for nothing that, according to Hamann, it turns out that the era of Impressionism is different
aestheticism of all areas of life; Hamann does not notice that he has attributed properties to facts
his aesthetic method. .
alive and alive

No. 9 BIBLIOGRAPHY. 167

Oh

style, as a material form, disappears and only what is common remains
for science, philosophy, morality and, for example, painting, i.e. ideology, social
consciousness. The result is primitive psychologism, pseudo-Marxist “ideology”
gism“, for which art, as a professional and material-organizing
category does not exist at all.

In the exact opposite position is Comrade. Zimmer. In a number of convincing
'his reasoning shows that to explain style by social worldviews
form is as absurd as the shape of an electric motor—individualistic psychology
capitalist. Unlike Haman-Frice, comrade. Zimmer strictly limits
the question of style as an independent aesthetic question, requiring independent
no other sociological explanation. For Comrade Zimmer understand social
the nature of artistic forms means not looking for their externally arbitrary similarity
ties with other types of culture, but to directly remove them from technology and
economics of society. Using examples of Romanesque, Gothic and Renaissance architecture,
textures, the author demonstrates how the material and artistic form determinesXia
socio-economic objectives and level of technology =

“History has shown us,” writes Comrade. Zimmer, only one
an example of a direct relationship between social ideology and style form.
It consists in the fact that public opinion can intervene in an already
existing forms of art and take the side of one of them (p. 370, becoming
infusing the dependence between the tasks of artistic construction and forms
his products, comrade Zimmer states: “the task itself stems from the ‘need’
society, and therefore it goes without saying that social ideology, spiritual
the state of a certain era has a greater or lesser influence on the particular
cultural character of more or less of these cultural needs. But
the way to accomplish the task depends on the degree of development of technology,
from the technical capabilities and skill that society has at its disposal,
than the concept of technology should be taken not in a narrow, but in a broader sense of the word,
which also contains artistic skill and experience" (p. 368). :

As is clear from the previous, the methodology defended by Comrade. Zimmer,
completely coincides with the ideas expressed and is largely justified
nymi, theorists of the so-called. production art. Therefore, only practically
The author’s ignorance can be explained by his attack against the production
parents or, as he unknowingly puts it, against the “cult of material.”

Despite this, the article by Comrade. Zimmer has a good justification for those
practical tasks that the leaders of the production movement set for themselves,
and a good blow to our dominant aesthetic ideologism.

year.

ciplines) was the main task of the team’s work during the 22-23 season
year. Ethe same task continues to be on the agenda now.

Changes in working methods took place only in the direction of closer
merging laboratory and production work.

so that the skills acquired in the process of laboratory work can be immediately
are also used in production work. This principle of close coordination
ity is currently receiving its further development and deepening, and

Denmark (direct orders and planned production tasks)
characters put forward by the studio itself).

Poster, caricature, illustration, popular print, inscription, slogan, playbill, advertising,

as before, areas of work' of the team.

production as a whole. The first steps in this direction were taken

“NOTE” AND “TIME” IN PROLETKULT.

At the “Spatial Arts Workshop” of Proletkult it was organized
the “NOTE” circle and the “Time” cell, registered in the “Time League”.

The "NOTE" circle aims to study the working conditions of the artist-producer.
property and its rationalization. By taking into account work skills, observation and
experiments, the circle strives to bring the work of the artist into the channels of rationalization, to
still living in the chaotic conditions of bohemia. The circle poses problems
labor, production and life of the artist. Strives to tighten working hours.
The head of both circles, N. Tarabukin, develops a card for registration
work and time, which will make it possible to draw conclusions not only on mathematics
rial obtained through observation and introspection, but also to use
statistical data. Similar problems applied to labor and production
staged by the artist for the first time and, despite their difficulty, due to complete
novelty of the issue are necessary attempts to move from studying only
physical labor to mental labor. ; b
